[30;1m2 | [0m[35mcreme is a library for incremental learning. Incremental learning is a machine learning regime[0m
[30;1m3 | [0m[35mwhere the observations are made available one by one. It is also known as online learning,[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35miterative learning, or sequential learning. This is in contrast to batch learning where all the[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35mdata is processed at once. Incremental learning is desirable when the data is too big to fit in[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35mmemory, or simply when it isn't available all at once. creme's API is heavily inspired from that of[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35mscikit-learn, enough so that users who are familiar with scikit-learn should feel right at home.[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35m"""[0m

[30;1m11 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m107 | [0m[35m[0m
